Current file excerpt/full content, possibly truncated:
```text
# Verdict
NEEDS_FIX

The final commit (`1aaa844`) genuinely closes the two hardest items from the prior two reviews: the probe is now cropped to the lookback+current window instead of copying the whole prefix (`_domain_probe_request`), and the gate now reuses cached probe scores instead of returning `{}`, which lets the router see stable probe evidence across consecutive consistency windows (`_cached_domain_probe_scores`). But the caching mechanism introduces a new, undocumented responsiveness cap in exactly the audio-only regime the probe exists to serve, the per-candidate audio re-encode flagged twice before is still unaddressed, and the primary acceptance criterion ("probes must not change the active inventory") is still only verified against `MockRetrieval`, which never swaps an index.

Evidence bound: `framework/agents/term_memory/topic_router.py` (`HybridWindowTopicRouter.observe`, `RouterConfig`, consistency logic) is **not in the packet**, and `omni.py` is truncated. Items 1 and 4 below depend on that router source and on unshown omni code; they are marked accordingly.

# Must fix before merge

### 1. Caching freezes the probe for `update_sec`, capping audio-only switch responsiveness
- **Severity:** Medium–High (in the audio-only fallback the probe is built for)
- **Where:** `framework/agents/omni.py` `_probe_domain_scores` — `last_domain_probe_at_s` is only written on a *fresh* probe; a fresh probe only runs when `update_gate` is false (`now - last_probe_at >= auto_glossary_update_sec`). Between fresh probes, `_cached_domain_probe_scores` returns the frozen scores.
- **Why real:** The fresh probe runs at most once per `update_sec` (production 30s). If the spoken topic changes shortly after a fresh probe (say audio flips ACL→medicine 2s after an NLP-scored probe), the probe signal stays "NLP" (cached) until the next fresh probe, up to ~28s later, then needs the 3-window audio-only consistency streak on top. In text mode this is masked because `text_topic_weight=0.60` updates every window from `router_text`; the freeze only bites the audio-only path — which is precisely the regime the docs say domain probes exist to cover ("When no source/ASR/topic text is available, the fallback should use small-top-k domain-probe retrieval"). The prior fix (caching) solved the consistency-window starvation by trading it for staleness, and the trade is undocumented. The docs claim caching yields "stable probe evidence"; they omit that it also blinds the probe to genuine mid-interval topic changes.
- **How to verify:** With `topic_router.py` in hand, drive `_process_batch`/`_probe_domain_scores` (mock) over ~20 audio-only segments with a topic flip 2s after a fresh probe; confirm the fresh probe (and thus any probe-driven switch) cannot occur until the next `update_sec` boundary.
- **Minimal fix direction:** Decouple probe refresh cadence from `update_sec` (refresh on the router's per-window consistency cadence, or cache only across the confirmation window, not the whole update interval), or explicitly document the audio-only responsiveness bound as `update_sec + consistency_windows`.

### 2. `_observe_active_glossary` is now `async`; full call-site coverage is unverifiable from the packet
- **Severity:** High if any un-awaited caller remains
- **Where:** `framework/agents/omni.py` `_observe_active_glossary` (now `async def`). The diff shows exactly one caller converted to `await`. `omni.py` is truncated, so I cannot confirm no other synchronous caller exists.
- **Why real:** A second un-awaited call yields a never-awaited coroutine (silently dropped observation, no test failure — only a `RuntimeWarning`). The passing test counts (41/18) do not exclude this.
- **How to verify:** `grep -n "_observe_active_glossary" framework/agents/omni.py`; confirm every call is awaited; run under `python -W error::RuntimeWarning`.

# Should fix

- **Per-candidate audio re-encode remains (flagged in both prior reviews, still not fixed).** `framework/agents/plugins/retrieval.py` `_probe_domain_scores_sync` calls `_retrieve_with_query_embeddings_sync([dict(request)], ...)` once per candidate slice; each call re-runs `_encode_audio_projected_seq_batch` on the *same* audio. The pooled audio embedding is identical across candidate indexes — only the text bank differs — so up to 4× redundant encodes (nlp/medicine/finance/legal) run under a single hold of `self._lock`, serialized against every session's main retrieval. The gate reduces frequency (~once per `update_sec`/session), not per-tick cost. Because `_process_batch` awaits `_probe_domain_scores` per session sequentially, a batch where many sessions' update windows align serializes N-candidate encodes × M sessions under the lock in one tick — a real retriever-GPU spike against the 32-session positioning in AGENTS.md. Minimal fix: encode the cropped window once per probe tick, score the single pooled embedding against each candidate text bank.
- **Dead request fields.** `_domain_probe_request` still passes `query_text` and `router_text_source`, which `_retrieve_with_query_embeddings_sync` ignores (probe is audio-only). Drop them or wire them; as-is they imply text-conditioned probing that does not happen.
- **Empty-scores gate bypass (narrow).** If a fresh probe ever returns `{}`, `last_domain_probe_at_s` is still set to `now`, so subsequent gated ticks hit an empty cache and fall through to a fresh probe every chunk, defeating the gate. In practice `probe_domain_scores` emits a `DomainProbeScore` per valid candidate regardless of reference count, so this is unlikely — but the fallthrough is unguarded.

# Missing tests / benchmarks

- **The core acceptance criterion is not tested against the code path that can violate it.** `test_domain_probe_populates_metadata_without_changing_active_inventory` uses `MockRetrieval.probe_domain_scores`, which never activates/swaps an index. The only component that mutates then restores the active index is `MaxSimRetrievalPlugin`, tested only in isolation (`test_probe_domain_scores_restores_active_index_and_threshold`), never end-to-end through `OmniAgent`. Nothing proves the agent's prompt references/top-k are invariant across a probe tick under the real swapping plugin — the exact failure mode the criterion guards against.
- **No integration test of the gate→cache→router→switch loop.** `test_domain_probe_reuses_cached_scores_inside_update_gate` proves cached scores are returned; `test_cached_probe_scores_can_confirm_audio_only_switch` proves the router switches on two hand-fed identical probes. Neither drives the omni gate over consecutive ticks to show cached scores actually reach the router and produce a switch, nor exercises the freeze in Must-fix #1.
- **`test_probe_assisted_scenarios_pass` cannot fail on probe quality.** `probe_for()` returns a hard-coded 0.9/0.8 matching the expected domain; it validates plumbing, not discrimination.

# Performance risks

- Serialized N-candidate audio re-encode under the retriever lock at each update tick (Should-fix above); worst case is batch-aligned update windows producing a per-batch GPU spike.

# Spec mismatch / surprise changes

- **The eval still does not exercise the wired path.** `eval_auto_glossary_switch.py` constructs `HybridWindowTopicRouter` directly with 2-D toy centroids/mock indexes, disables hysteresis (`update_interval_sec=0.0`, `switch_cooldown_sec=0.0`), applies switches instantly (ignoring the `is_index_ready` preload gate), and fabricates probe scores; it never calls `OmniAgent._probe_domain_scores` or `MaxSimRetrievalPlugin.probe_domain_scores`. So the reported "ACL→medicine 4 / medicine→ACL 2 windows" characterize the pre-existing text-topic router with hysteresis off, not this patch's probe wiring. **This is materially mitigated** in the final commit: the docstring and `docs/*` now explicitly label it "router-unit diagnostic… not an end-to-end proof of live ASR, Omni batch-loop timing, real MaxSim domain-probe quality, or production switch latency," and the README entry says "diagnostic." Remaining surprise: the README/`docs` still cite these window counts as run results without stating the numbers are hysteresis-disabled/synthetic-probe at the point of citation.
- **`--max-windows-per-domain 8` line slicing.** The medicine source file reportedly opens with non-medical webinar/operator lines, so the "4-window" real-text latency partly reflects arbitrary first-8-line selection, not router responsiveness. Docs acknowledge this narratively.

# Possible false positives (do not re-raise)

- **Fixed since review #1/#2:** full-prefix copy → now cropped `[start:end]` (`_domain_probe_request`, confirmed by `test_domain_probe_request_uses_recent_audio_window`); 0.78 threshold suppression → `score_threshold=None`; probe-every-chunk → gated by warmup/update/cooldown.
- Plugin restore logic (`old_index`, `old_threshold`, `missing` sentinel) is correct and runs under `self._lock`; no data race with main retrieval, no risk of leaving the wrong active index.
- `_activate_sync` is a cached-tensor pointer swap; index *loading* is not the cost — the cost is the repeated encode+matmul.
- `domain_probe_top_k` plumbing (yaml → `OmniConfig` → `_topic_meta`) and the `domain_probe_cached`/`domain_probe_s` metadata additions are internally consistent; not bugs. Caching correctly does *not* advance `last_domain_probe_at_s`.

# Final recommendation

Do not merge as-is. Before merge: (1) address the audio-only probe freeze in Must-fix #1 — either refresh the probe on the router's consistency cadence rather than `update_sec`, or document the `update_sec`-bounded audio-only latency; (2) confirm every `_observe_active_glossary` call site awaits the now-async method; (3) add an agent-level test that runs a probe tick through the *real* `MaxSimRetrievalPlugin` swap path and asserts active-inventory/prompt-top-k invariance, plus a consecutive-tick test that shows the gated cache actually drives a switch through the omni loop; and (4) encode the cropped audio once per probe tick instead of once per candidate. Items 1 and 2 cannot be fully confirmed without `framework/agents/term_memory/topic_router.py` and the untruncated `omni.py`.
```

```text
# Verdict
NEEDS_FIX

The final commit (`34f5e3f`) does two real things on top of the previously-reviewed branch: it rewrites the probe to encode the audio window **once** and score it against each candidate text bank (`_encode_probe_window_sync` + a matmul loop in `_probe_domain_scores_sync`), which genuinely closes the per-candidate re-encode flagged in the earlier passes; and it adds `_domain_probe_refresh_sec` so audio-only sessions refresh probes on the window cadence instead of freezing for `update_sec`, which closes the audio-only consistency-starvation/freeze from the prior pass. But the freeze fix reintroduces a per-chunk retriever-GPU cost in the *only regime that actually ships today* (no ASR producer → `router_text_source == "none"` always → audio-only cadence), the sync→async `_observe_active_glossary` conversion is still unverifiable from the packet, and the cooldown gate depends on a `last_switch_s` clock that is not shown.

Evidence bounds: `framework/agents/omni.py` is truncated and `framework/agents/term_memory/topic_router.py` (RouterConfig / `observe` / `last_switch_s` semantics) is **not in the packet**. Items 2 and 4 depend on those.

# Must fix before merge

### 1. In the shipping (no-ASR) configuration the probe runs a fresh audio encode on ~every chunk, per session, under the retriever lock
- **Severity:** Medium–High (throughput regression against the concurrency positioning)
- **Where:** `framework/agents/omni.py` `_domain_probe_refresh_sec` (audio-only branch returns `base_segment_sec * latency_multiplier` ≈ one segment) and `_probe_domain_scores` (fresh-probe path calls `retrieval.probe_domain_scores` → `_encode_probe_window_sync`); called per session inside the `_process_batch` loop.
- **Why real:** The task packet states this patch ships **no** real streaming ASR producer, so in live deployment `router_text_source` is `"none"` and `router_text_window` is empty for every session. `_domain_probe_refresh_sec` then always returns the window cadence, so `update_gate` (`now - last_probe_at < refresh_sec`) is false roughly every other window and a **fresh** probe runs. Each fresh probe re-runs `_encode_audio_projected_seq_batch` + `_multiscale_pool` on the window — the same audio encode the main retrieval already did for that chunk — so audio-only sessions pay ~2× the retriever audio-encode per chunk. `probe_domain_scores` holds `self._lock`, which mutually excludes the main `retrieve_with_metadata`, and `_probe_domain_scores` is awaited sequentially per session in the batch loop, so N sessions serialize N extra encodes per tick on the retriever GPU. The earlier "gate on `update_sec`" only cheapens the *text* regime, which does not exist yet. Net: the gating that the docs credit for making this cheap is inert in the configuration that actually runs, directly against the 32-sessions/GPU framing in AGENTS.md.
- **How to verify:** Count `_encode_probe_window_sync` / `_encode_audio_projected_seq_batch` calls per chunk for an audio-only mock/real session over ~20 segments (expect roughly one extra encode per 1–2 windows), and measure `domain_probe_s` vs `retrieve_s` under multiple concurrent audio-only sessions.
- **Minimal fix direction:** Reuse the pooled window embedding already computed by the main retrieval pass for that chunk (it is discarded today) instead of re-encoding inside the probe; or cap audio-only probe cadence to a multiple of the segment and document the resulting switch-latency bound. Either way, do not double-encode the same window per chunk.

### 2. `_observe_active_glossary` became `async`; full call-site coverage cannot be confirmed
- **Severity:** High if any un-awaited caller remains
- **Where:** `framework/agents/omni.py` `_observe_active_glossary` (now `async def`); the diff converts exactly one caller to `await`.
- **Why real:** A second, un-awaited call yields a never-awaited coroutine — the observation is silently dropped with only a `RuntimeWarning`, which the passing unit counts (19) would not catch. `omni.py` is truncated, so I cannot confirm this is the only caller.
- **How to verify:** `grep -n "_observe_active_glossary" framework/agents/omni.py`; confirm every call is awaited; run under `python -W error::RuntimeWarning`.

# Should fix

- **Cooldown gate depends on an unshown clock.** `_probe_domain_scores` computes `cooldown_gate` from `now - float(state.last_switch_s)` with `now = time.perf_counter()`. If the omni switch-application path sets `state.last_switch_s` in any other domain (wall clock, segment index), the cooldown gate is meaningless or permanently open. `topic_router.py` and the omni switch-apply code are not in the packet, so this cannot be confirmed. Verify `last_switch_s` is written with `time.perf_counter()`.
- **`domain_probe_s` is stale on cached chunks.** `_cached_domain_probe_scores` sets `last_domain_probe_cached = True` but does not touch `last_domain_probe_s`, so the emitted `domain_probe_s` on a cached chunk reports the *previous fresh* probe's latency, not this chunk's (which was ~0). A latency consumer must gate on `domain_probe_cached`; otherwise the metric over-reports. Either zero it on cache or document the coupling.
- **Empty-fresh-probe still bypasses the gate.** If a fresh probe returns `{}` (e.g., `_encode_probe_window_sync` returns `None` on a short/degenerate window), `last_domain_probe_at_s = now` is set but `last_domain_probe_raw_scores = {}`, so the next gated tick finds an empty cache and re-probes. Harmless in the audio-only cadence, but in text mode it defeats the 30s gate until a non-empty probe. Guard the empty case.
- **Dead request fields.** `_domain_probe_request` still passes `query_text` and `router_text_source`, which the audio-only encode path (`_encode_probe_window_sync`) ignores. Drop them or wire them; as-is they imply a text-conditioned probe that does not happen.

# Missing tests / benchmarks

- No benchmark measures the per-chunk probe cost under concurrent audio-only sessions — the exact regime this commit makes per-window (Must-fix #1). The perf claim in the docs is unmeasured.
- The core acceptance criterion ("probes must not change the active inventory / prompt top-10") is still only asserted against `MockRetrieval` (`test_domain_probe_populates_metadata_without_changing_active_inventory`), which never swaps an index. The only component that mutates+restores the active index is `MaxSimRetrievalPlugin`; its restore is tested in isolation (`test_probe_domain_scores_scores_candidates_without_activating_indexes`) but never end-to-end through `OmniAgent`. Note the new plugin `_probe_domain_scores_sync` no longer calls `activate_index` at all (it reads `_ensure_index(...)` directly and matmuls), so index mutation is now structurally avoided — but no agent-level test proves prompt refs/top-k are invariant across a probe tick under the real plugin.
- `test_domain_probe_refresh_uses_window_cadence_without_text` asserts the helper returns 1.92 vs 30.0, but nothing drives the omni loop over consecutive audio-only ticks to show the per-window fresh probe actually reaches the router and produces a switch (only the router-side `test_cached_probe_scores_can_confirm_audio_only_switch` with hand-fed identical probes does).
- `test_probe_assisted_scenarios_pass` / `probe_for()` return a hard-coded 0.9/0.8 matching the expected domain and cannot fail on probe discrimination.

# Performance risks

- Must-fix #1: doubled audio encode per chunk for audio-only sessions, serialized under `self._lock`, N sessions sequentially per batch tick — retriever-GPU bound (not on the vLLM TP path, so no TP/PP interaction, but a real serialization point). The repo's own `auto_glossary_routing_probe_20260707.md` characterizes the domain-probe retrieval-score signal as "too noisy by itself" (medicine top-score delta ~0.01), so this per-chunk cost buys a 0.25-weighted signal of contested value in the audio-only regime.

# Spec mismatch / surprise changes

- The `eval_auto_glossary_switch.py` "switch latency 2/4 windows" numbers still come from a direct `HybridWindowTopicRouter` unit with `update_interval_sec=0.0`/`switch_cooldown_sec=0.0`, instant `apply_switch` (no `is_index_ready` preload gate), 2-D toy centroids, and fabricated `probe_for()` scores; it never calls `OmniAgent._probe_domain_scores` or `MaxSimRetrievalPlugin.probe_domain_scores`. This is **materially mitigated** in this commit: the docstring, README ("diagnostic"), and `docs/*` now explicitly label it "router-unit diagnostic … not an end-to-end proof of live ASR, Omni batch-loop timing, real MaxSim domain-probe quality, or production switch latency." Remaining surprise: the docs still cite the window counts as run results at the point of citation without repeating the "hysteresis-disabled / synthetic-probe" caveat inline.
- `--max-windows-per-domain 8` first-N-line slicing of the medicine source (which opens with non-medical operator/webinar lines) partly drives the "4-window" real-text latency; docs acknowledge this narratively.

# Possible false positives (do not re-raise)

- **Fixed in this commit — do not re-raise:** per-candidate audio re-encode (now single encode in `_encode_probe_window_sync`, one matmul per candidate text bank); full-prefix copy (now cropped `[start:end]`, confirmed by `test_domain_probe_request_uses_recent_audio_window`); 0.78-threshold suppression (`score_threshold=None`); audio-only probe freeze (now window-cadence refresh).
- The plugin probe no longer activates/swaps the active index at all (`_probe_domain_scores_sync` reads text banks via `_ensure_index` and matmuls locally, under `self._lock`), so there is no active-index-mutation risk and no data race with main retrieval on that path.
- `domain_probe_top_k` plumbing (yaml → `OmniConfig` → `_topic_meta`) and the `domain_probe_cached`/`domain_probe_s` metadata additions are internally consistent; caching correctly does not advance `last_domain_probe_at_s`.

# Final recommendation

Do not merge as-is. Before merge: (1) stop re-encoding the same window in the probe — reuse the pooled embedding the main retrieval already computes, or bound and document the audio-only probe cadence/cost (Must-fix #1); (2) confirm every `_observe_active_glossary` call site awaits the now-async method (Must-fix #2); (3) confirm `state.last_switch_s` is written in the `perf_counter` domain the cooldown gate assumes; and (4) add an agent-level test asserting prompt-refs/top-k invariance across a probe tick through the real `MaxSimRetrievalPlugin`, plus a concurrency/latency measurement of the per-chunk probe under multiple audio-only sessions. Items 2 and 3 cannot be fully confirmed without the untruncated `omni.py` and `topic_router.py`.
```

```text
# Verdict
NEEDS_FIX

This is the fifth pass (`6d736b5`). It genuinely closes the one remaining hard performance item from pass four: the probe no longer re-encodes audio per chunk — it reuses the mean-pooled `query_embedding` the main retrieval already produced (`_probe_window_embeddings_from_request`), falling back to `_encode_probe_window_sync` only when no pooled embedding exists. But that reuse introduces a new, untested semantic divergence in probe scoring, the shipping (no-ASR) config's audio-only switch reachability is still unverifiable and plausibly inert, and the async-caller/metric/gate items flagged earlier remain.

Evidence bounds: `framework/agents/term_memory/topic_router.py` (`RouterConfig`, `HybridWindowTopicRouter.observe`, score normalization, `last_switch_s` semantics) is **not in the packet**, and `omni.py` is truncated. Items 2, 3, and 4 depend on that source and are marked accordingly.

# Must fix before merge

### 1. Reusing the mean-pooled query embedding changes probe scoring from multi-window MaxSim to a single-vector dot product, and diverges from the fallback path
- **Severity:** Medium (correctness/consistency of the signal this whole change exists to feed)
- **Where:** `framework/agents/plugins/retrieval.py` `_probe_window_embeddings_from_request` (consumes `request["query_embedding"]`) vs `_encode_probe_window_sync` (fallback); `_probe_domain_scores_sync` does `scores_t = window_embs.matmul(text_embs.T).max(dim=0).values`.
- **Why real:** The reused `query_embedding` is the **mean-pooled, single** vector computed in `_retrieve_with_query_embeddings_sync` (`pooled = window_embs[row_valid].mean(dim=0)`), so `_probe_window_embeddings_from_request` yields shape `[1, D]` and the probe's `.max(dim=0)` over one row is just `pooled · term`. The fallback `_encode_probe_window_sync` instead returns `window_embs[valid_windows]` (shape `[N_windows, D]`), so the probe there is a genuine per-window MaxSim (`max_w window_w · term`). These are not the same statistic: mean-then-dot washes out the per-window peaks that MaxSim is designed to surface, and typically produces lower, blurrier scores. So the probe's `top_score`/`mean_topk_score` now depend on **which path ran** (pooled reuse vs re-encode) — inconsistent scoring for the same audio. The repo's own `auto_glossary_routing_probe_20260707.md` already characterizes the domain-probe signal as "too noisy by itself" (~0.01 medicine-vs-NLP delta); blurring it through mean-pooling can only weaken it further.
- **How to verify:** On one real medicine window, compute the probe with the reused pooled vector vs with the multi-window encode, against the nlp/medicine banks; compare `top_score` and the medicine-vs-nlp delta. Confirm the two paths rank domains identically.
- **Minimal fix direction:** Either carry the per-window embeddings (not just the pooled mean) from the main retrieval for reuse, or accept the pooled vector only as an explicit approximation and document that the probe statistic differs from MaxSim; do not silently mix a single-vector path and a multi-window path under the same `DomainProbeScore` fields.

### 2. `_observe_active_glossary` is now `async`; full call-site coverage still cannot be confirmed
- **Severity:** High if any un-awaited caller remains
- **Where:** `framework/agents/omni.py` `_observe_active_glossary` (`async def`); the diff converts exactly one caller to `await`.
- **Why real:** A second un-awaited call yields a never-awaited coroutine — the observation is silently dropped with only a `RuntimeWarning`, which the passing `19 passed` counts would not catch. `omni.py` is truncated so I cannot confirm this is the only caller. This has been unresolved across all prior passes.
- **How to verify:** `grep -n "_observe_active_glossary" framework/agents/omni.py`; confirm every call is awaited; run under `python -W error::RuntimeWarning`.

# Should fix

- **Audio-only switching may be unreachable in the shipping config (probe inert where it matters).** The task packet states no ASR producer ships, so `router_text_source == "none"` and `text_topic_weight` (0.60) contributes nothing in production. The remaining weights sum to `domain_probe(0.25) + speech_centroid(0.10) + metadata_prior(0.05) = 0.40`, below `min_confidence = 0.60`. The packet's own `test_cached_probe_scores_can_confirm_audio_only_switch` only switches after setting `domain_probe_weight=1.0` and `min_confidence=0.5` — i.e. it does **not** exercise production weights. If the router applies `min_confidence` against this weighted sum without renormalization, audio-only probe-driven switching can never fire in the config that actually runs, making the entire wired probe machinery inert in deployment. This cannot be confirmed without `topic_router.py`; it should be resolved or explicitly stated.
- **`domain_probe_s` is stale on cached chunks.** `_cached_domain_probe_scores` sets `last_domain_probe_cached=True` and `last_domain_probe_s=0.0` — good — but the fresh-probe latency reporting still requires a consumer to gate on `domain_probe_cached`. This is now correct in code (`0.0` on cache); confirm the UI/latency consumer does not average cached `0.0` into a p50/p95 as if it were a real measurement.
- **Empty-fresh-probe still bypasses the gate.** If a fresh probe returns `{}` (e.g., `_encode_probe_window_sync` returns `None` on a degenerate/short window), `_probe_domain_scores` sets `last_domain_probe_at_s = now` but `last_domain_probe_raw_scores = {}`, so the next gated tick finds an empty cache and re-probes. Harmless in the per-window audio-only cadence, but in text mode it defeats the update-interval gate until a non-empty probe.
- **Dead request fields.** `_domain_probe_request` no longer passes `query_text`/`router_text_source` in this HEAD (it passes `audio_buffer`, the three time fields, and `query_embedding`) — confirm no downstream reader still expects the removed fields.

# Missing tests / benchmarks

- No test exercises the **pooled-reuse vs re-encode divergence** (Must-fix #1): `test_probe_domain_scores_scores_candidates_without_activating_indexes` feeds a hand-built single `[1.0, 0.0]` vector and forces the encode path to raise, so it validates plumbing, not the multi-window/pooled equivalence.
- No agent-level test proves prompt references/top-k are invariant across a probe tick through the **real** `MaxSimRetrievalPlugin`; the invariance test uses `MockRetrieval`, which never swaps an index. Note the plugin probe now reads banks via `_ensure_index` + matmul and does not call `activate_index`, so the mutation risk is structurally reduced — but still unasserted through the agent.
- No concurrency/latency measurement of the per-chunk probe (matmul-under-lock) with multiple audio-only sessions; the perf claim remains unmeasured (now cheaper, but still per-chunk under `self._lock`).
- `test_probe_assisted_scenarios_pass` / `probe_for()` return a hard-coded 0.9/0.8 matching the expected domain and cannot fail on probe discrimination.

# Performance risks

- The dominant re-encode regression is resolved for the common path (pooled reuse). Residual: `probe_domain_scores` still holds `self._lock` and runs N candidate matmuls per probe tick, serialized against every session's main retrieval; cheap per-op, but per-chunk in the shipping audio-only cadence and serialized across sessions in the batch loop. The fallback `_encode_probe_window_sync` reintroduces a full re-encode whenever `query_embedding` is None (degenerate windows) — bounded, but present.

# Spec mismatch / surprise changes

- The `eval_auto_glossary_switch.py` "ACL→medicine 4 / medicine→ACL 2 windows" numbers still come from a direct `HybridWindowTopicRouter` unit with `update_interval_sec=0.0`/`switch_cooldown_sec=0.0`, instant `apply_switch` (no `is_index_ready` preload gate), 2-D toy centroids, and synthetic `probe_for()`; it never calls `OmniAgent._probe_domain_scores` or `MaxSimRetrievalPlugin.probe_domain_scores`. This is **materially mitigated** — the docstring, README ("diagnostic"), and `docs/*` now explicitly label it "router-unit diagnostic … not an end-to-end proof of live ASR, Omni batch-loop timing, real MaxSim domain-probe quality, or production switch latency." Remaining surprise: the docs still cite the window counts as run results at the point of citation without repeating the hysteresis-disabled/synthetic-probe caveat inline.
- `--max-windows-per-domain 8` first-N-line slicing of the medicine source (opens with non-medical operator/webinar lines) partly drives the real-text "4-window" latency; docs acknowledge this narratively.

# Possible false positives (do not re-raise)
- **Fixed in this commit:** per-chunk audio re-encode (now reuses the main retrieval's pooled embedding; `test_..._reuses_the_main_retrieval query_embedding` asserts the encode path is not hit). Also previously fixed and confirmed: full-prefix copy → cropped `[start:end]`; 0.78 threshold suppression → `score_threshold=None`; ungated per-chunk probe → warmup/update/cooldown gating; audio-only freeze → per-window cadence.
- The plugin probe no longer activates/swaps the active index (`_probe_domain_scores_sync` reads banks via `_ensure_index` and matmuls under `self._lock`), so there is no active-index-mutation risk or data race with main retrieval on that path.
- `domain_probe_top_k` plumbing (yaml → `OmniConfig` → `_topic_meta`) and `domain_probe_cached`/`domain_probe_s` metadata are internally consistent; caching correctly does not advance `last_domain_probe_at_s`.

# Final recommendation
Do not merge as-is. Before merge: (1) reconcile the probe scoring statistic — reuse per-window embeddings (not the mean-pooled vector) or explicitly document/measure that the pooled approximation ranks domains equivalently, so the fast and fallback paths agree (Must-fix #1); (2) confirm every `_observe_active_glossary` call site awaits the now-async method (Must-fix #2); (3) resolve or explicitly state whether audio-only switching is reachable under production weights (`0.40 < min_confidence 0.60`) in the no-ASR config that ships. Items 2, 3, and the audio-only-reachability question cannot be fully confirmed without `framework/agents/term_memory/topic_router.py` and the untruncated `omni.py`.
```

## .codex/reviews/claude-review-20260706-204908.md

Current file excerpt/full content, possibly truncated:
```text
# Verdict
NEEDS_FIX

The change under review is `6d736b5 → 8a911aa` ("Preserve window probe routing semantics"): it (a) carries per-window speech embeddings from the main retrieval pass into the domain probe so probe scoring is genuine multi-window MaxSim instead of a mean-pooled dot product, (b) renormalizes the router score over the signals actually present in a window, and (c) makes `common_10k` an explicit working preset. (a) and (c) look correct and are tested. (b) is a real semantic change to the documented score/confidence gate that amplifies a signal the repo itself calls "too noisy," and the regression that would expose a resulting false switch is not exercised. There is also an AGENTS-violating/self-inconsistent doc path.

# Must fix before merge

### 1. Weight renormalization inflates single-signal confidence toward 1.0, weakening the `min_confidence` gate on the audio-only probe path
- **Severity:** Medium–High (correctness/robustness of the switch decision; hidden regression risk)
- **Where:** `framework/agents/term_memory/topic_router.py` `_score_hybrid` — `active_weight_sum` and `conf = weighted / active_weight_sum`.
- **Why real:** When only one signal is active, `active_weight_sum` equals that signal's own weight, so `conf = weight*normalized_top / weight = normalized_top`. In the shipping (no-ASR) config `router_text_source == "none"`, so the audio-only regime routinely has just the probe active (or probe + a weak centroid). A lone, top-normalized probe therefore drives `conf` to ~1.0 and clears `min_confidence=0.60` — the exact gate the README/docs describe as "minimum router confidence to switch." This is precisely what made audio-only switching reachable (the prior pass's `0.40 < 0.60` complaint), but it does so by amplifying the domain-probe signal that `docs/auto_glossary_routing_probe_20260707.md` characterizes as "too noisy by itself" (medicine-vs-NLP top-score delta ~0.01). The only remaining guards are `min_margin=0.15` and the 3-window audio-only consistency streak; the confidence gate no longer meaningfully constrains audio-only switches.
- **How to verify:** Drive `_score_hybrid`/`observe` audio-only (no `router_text`) with a *multi-domain* probe dict where the wrong domain is marginally higher on a few consecutive windows (the ACL-window-predicts-medicine 3/13 case the probe doc reports), using production weights and `min_confidence=0.60`. Confirm whether a false switch fires. The existing `test_audio_only_probe_requires_three_consistent_windows` feeds a single-domain probe dict (`{"medicine": ...}` only), which yields an artificial full margin and cannot surface this.
- **Minimal fix direction:** Either keep the renormalization but reinstate an absolute-evidence floor on the probe-only regime (e.g., require raw probe `top_score` / margin above an explicit threshold before it can reach switch confidence), or add an audio-only ACL-only regression with a realistic multi-domain noisy probe asserting `switch_count == 0`. Do not present a renormalized single-signal score as "confidence" against the documented 0.60 gate without such a guard/test.

### 2. Audio-only probe behavior — the regime this whole change targets — is still not validated with realistic probes
- **Severity:** Medium (benchmark/spec validity)
- **Where:** docs cite `..._final7.json` and `/tmp/auto_glossary_switch_fixture_probe_final7.json`; test log shows the `--with-probe` run uses synthetic `probe_for()` (0.9/0.8 matching the expected domain) and the real-source run uses `router_text_source=manifest_source` (text path, `with_probe=false`).
- **Why real:** The renormalization specifically changes the *audio-only, probe-driven* path. Neither cited "final7" run exercises it: one is text/keyword-driven, the other feeds hand-tuned single-domain synthetic probes. So "passed all four router-unit scenarios / zero false switches" is evidence for the text path, not for the newly-reachable renormalized probe path. The docs present these as the validation for this change.
- **How to verify:** Grep the eval — `probe_for()` returns a fixed 0.9/0.8 for the expected domain only; no realistic multi-domain probe or noisy ACL medicine-leakage case is fed.
- **Minimal fix direction:** Add a probe-only scenario with contested per-window scores (both domains scored, wrong domain occasionally higher) and assert no false switch; or explicitly state in the docs that audio-only renormalized-probe switching is unvalidated.

# Should fix

- **Doc path is non-host-qualified and inconsistent with its own command block (AGENTS.md violation).** `docs/adaptive_working_glossary.md` / `adaptive_working_glossary_eval.md` / `auto_glossary_routing_probe_20260707.md` prose cite `/mnt/data2/jiaxuanluo/rasst-demo/runtime/eval/..._final7.json`, but the command block immediately above writes to `/mnt/taurus/data2/jiaxuanluo/.../auto_glossary_switch_router_only_20260707.json`. AGENTS.md requires host-qualified Taurus paths and forbids bare `/mnt/...` non-Taurus paths in docs. The prose references a different, bare path than the documented command produces, so the "run" is not reproducible from the doc. Also `/tmp/...final7.json` is an ephemeral, non-reproducible location being cited as evidence.
- **Per-request window-matrix CPU transfer on the hot path even when unused.** `retrieval.py` `_retrieve_with_query_embeddings_sync` now does `valid_window_embs.detach().cpu().float()` and stores it on every `RetrievalResult` for every request every chunk, but it is only consumed when a gated probe fires. It is small (~N_windows×D), but it is an unconditional extra device→host copy added for all sessions/chunks against the concurrency positioning; gate it or accept it explicitly.
- **`_retrieve_slice_groups` gained a required positional param.** Both shown call sites (main + rescue) are updated; `omni.py` is truncated so a third caller cannot be excluded from the packet. A missing arg is a hard `TypeError` (not silent), so lower risk than the prior async concern, but confirm `grep -n "_retrieve_slice_groups" framework/agents/omni.py` shows only the two updated sites.
- **Reuse path silently ignores `_domain_probe_request`'s own audio window.** When the reused `query_embedding` (window matrix) is present, `_probe_window_embeddings_from_request` returns it and the probe never uses the request's `audio_buffer`/`current_*_sec`. Scoring the main-retrieval window is arguably correct, but the still-present `_domain_probe_request`/`_domain_probe_refresh_sec` audio machinery now only matters on the fallback (no-embedding) path — document this so the two windows are not assumed identical.

# Missing tests / benchmarks

- No test with a **realistic multi-domain noisy probe** on the audio-only path (item 1) — the single-domain probe dicts in `test_hybrid_window_topic_router` and `test_auto_working_fixed_top10` create an unrealistically clean margin.
- No agent-level test that a probe tick leaves prompt refs/top-k invariant **through the real `MaxSimRetrievalPlugin`**; the invariance test still uses `MockRetrieval`, which never sets `query_window_embeddings` or swaps a bank. The multi-window MaxSim reuse is tested only at the plugin unit level (`test_probe_domain_scores_scores_candidates_without_activating_indexes`).
- No measurement of the extra per-chunk window-matrix transfer / probe cost under concurrent audio-only sessions.

# Performance risks

- Unconditional per-request per-chunk `.cpu()` of the window embedding matrix for all sessions (Should-fix above); small per-op but on the retriever hot path for every request whether or not a probe consumes it.

# Spec mismatch / surprise changes

- The score formula documented as fixed weights `0.60/0.25/0.10/0.05` now renormalizes over present signals, changing what `confidence`/`min_confidence` mean (item 1). Docs were updated to mention renormalization, but not the consequence that a single active signal saturates confidence and effectively bypasses the 0.60 gate.
- Commit title "Preserve window probe routing semantics" preserves the *MaxSim window* semantics of the probe (correctly), but simultaneously *changes* the router scoring/confidence semantics via renormalization; the title undersells the second, riskier change.

# Possible false positives (do not re-raise)

- The mean-pool-vs-MaxSim divergence flagged in the prior pass is genuinely fixed here: `query_window_embeddings` carries the already-`F.normalize`d per-window rows, and `_probe_window_embeddings_from_request` + `.max(dim=0)` yields true multi-window MaxSim consistent with the `_encode_probe_window_sync` fallback. `test_retrieval_plugin` now feeds a 2-window `[[1,0],[0,1]]` query and asserts the correct window-2 term, exercising this.
- `RetrievalResult.query_window_embeddings` inserted between existing fields is safe — all instantiations use keyword args.
- `WORKING_GLOSSARY_PRESETS` now including `common_10k` does not make it a routing target: `_domain_slices_for` still iterates `configured_working_presets(auto_glossary_presets)` (the 4 domain presets) and skips general/common; the addition only enables the mock base-slice path in `active_glossary._describe` and the base+overlay builder. `test_auto_active_retrieval_uses_common_base_plus_domain_overlay` confirms `[common_10k, nlp_core_10k]` / `[base, domain]`.
- Text-present path is ~unchanged: with all signals active the denominator ≈ 1.0, so renormalization is near-identity there.

# Final recommendation

Do not merge as-is. Before merge: (1) constrain the renormalized audio-only probe path so a lone normalized signal cannot clear `min_confidence` on the noisy probe evidence the repo's own doc distrusts — or add an audio-only, multi-domain, noisy-probe ACL-only regression asserting zero false switches; (2) stop citing text-path/synthetic-probe "final7" runs as validation for the renormalized audio-only probe behavior, and add a realistic probe-only case; (3) fix the non-host-qualified/self-inconsistent doc paths per AGENTS.md. The per-window MaxSim reuse (the headline fix) is sound; the renormalization is the item to gate. Items depending on the truncated `omni.py` (`_retrieve_slice_groups` caller completeness, `_probe_domain_scores` threading of the window embedding into the request) cannot be fully confirmed from the packet.

```

```text
# Verdict
LOOKS_OK_WITH_RISKS

The change under review is `8a911aa → df1401b` ("Guard audio-only domain probe switches"): it adds three config fields (`audio_probe_min_top_score=0.50`, `audio_probe_min_raw_margin=0.08`, `audio_probe_min_positive_domains=2`) plumbed yaml → `OmniConfig` → `RouterConfig`, a `_audio_probe_guard` helper in `HybridWindowTopicRouter`, a new guard branch (`audio_probe_evidence_insufficient`) that fires only on the `not has_text and has_probe` path, and gates the per-request `query_window_embeddings` CPU transfer behind `return_query_window_embeddings` (set from `session.auto_glossary_enabled`). This is the direct answer to the prior pass's Must-fix (renormalization letting a lone normalized probe clear `min_confidence`). The diff is scoped, the text path is untouched, and the two failure modes are now unit-tested. No regression is introduced. Residual gaps below are real but narrow, and consistent with the docs' "guarded fallback" framing.

# Must fix before merge
None that are hard blockers in this diff.

# Should fix

### 1. Centroid-only audio-only path still bypasses the new guard
- **Severity:** Medium (correctness gap in exactly the regime this commit claims to guard)
- **Where:** `framework/agents/term_memory/topic_router.py` `HybridWindowTopicRouter.observe` — `elif not has_text and has_probe and not audio_probe_guard.get("ok", False)`.
- **Why real:** The new guard is gated on `has_probe`. When audio-only (`not has_text`) has **no** positive probe (`has_probe` False) but a query embedding / EMA centroid is present, `_score_hybrid` renormalizes over the lone centroid signal so `conf ≈ normalized_top`, which can clear `min_confidence=0.60` — the exact confidence-inflation the guard exists to stop, just via the centroid instead of the probe. The repo's own `docs/auto_glossary_routing_probe_20260707.md` calls the centroid non-discriminative ("medicine windows closer to the NLP centroid"), so this is the signal most likely to false-switch. In the shipping config the probe usually returns positive cosine scores so `has_probe` is normally True; the gap bites only when the probe encode is empty/degenerate — narrow, but it is the same class of bug that was just "fixed."
- **How to verify:** Drive `observe` audio-only with `domain_probe_scores={}` and a strong wrong-domain `query_embedding` over ≥ consistency windows under production weights (`min_confidence=0.60`); check whether a switch fires with no raw-evidence gate.
- **Minimal fix direction:** Extend the guard trigger to the audio-only-no-text case regardless of `has_probe` (require an absolute evidence floor before any lone renormalized audio signal reaches switch confidence), or block audio-only switching entirely when `not has_probe`.

### 2. `min_positive_domains=2` couples the guard to "≥2 candidate domains scored positive"
- **Severity:** Low
- **Where:** `_audio_probe_guard` `ok` computation.
- **Why real:** The prior single-domain probe tests (`test_audio_only_probe_requires_three_consistent_windows`, `test_cached_probe_scores_can_confirm_audio_only_switch`) had to add a second `nlp` probe entry to keep passing, which shows the guard rejects a genuinely strong single-domain audio signal when only one candidate index is positive. Default config scores 4 domain slices so this is fine, but a deployment that preloads only the current + one target domain (`auto_glossary_preload_presets`) can silently make audio-only switching unreachable. Document the assumption or key the floor off the target/runner-up pair rather than a raw positive count.

### 3. Given measured ~0.01 real probe deltas, `min_raw_margin=0.08` likely makes audio-only switching inert in production
- **Severity:** Low (design/spec, documented)
- **Where:** guard threshold vs `docs/auto_glossary_routing_probe_20260707.md` ("Avg medicine top-score delta 0.0112 / -0.0461").
- **Why real:** The doc's own real-audio measurements put the medicine-vs-NLP raw top-score margin around/below 0.01–0.05, well under the 0.08 gate, so the guarded audio-only probe will almost never fire on real audio. Combined with the shipped scope having no ASR producer (text path also inert), the router effectively pins the initial preset in deployment. The docs acknowledge this ("remains a guarded fallback rather than the main production signal"), so this is not a bug, but the eval evidence (§ below) should not be read as demonstrating a working audio-only production switch.

# Missing tests / benchmarks
- No agent-level test exercises the new `return_query_window_embeddings` request flag through the real `MaxSimRetrievalPlugin` and asserts the probe consumes per-window embeddings; the invariance/probe tests still use `MockRetrieval`, which never sets `query_window_embeddings`. So the gating change (window matrix now only transferred for auto sessions) is verified only by reading the diff, not by a test.
- No test covers the centroid-only audio-only path (Should-fix #1) — the exact case the guard leaves open.
- The audio-only guard is validated only at the router-unit level with synthetic probes (`test_audio_only_contested_probe_...`, and the `--router-text-source none --with-probe` fixture run in the log). That is adequate for the state-machine, but there is still no run where a *real* MaxSim probe over real ACL/medicine audio drives (or correctly refuses) an audio-only switch, so the guard's thresholds are unvalidated against real deltas.

# Performance risks
- Gating `query_window_embeddings` behind `return_query_window_embeddings` removes the prior unconditional per-request device→host copy for non-auto sessions — a small improvement, not a risk. `_audio_probe_guard` runs on every `observe` (including the text path) and does an O(#domains) sort/scan; with ≤4 domains this is negligible.

# Spec mismatch / surprise changes
- The documented fixed-weight formula (`0.60/0.25/0.10/0.05`) plus renormalization plus the new raw-evidence guard are now all reflected in `docs/adaptive_working_glossary.md`, and the switch-guard ordering doc lists the new guard. No undocumented behavior change in this diff.
- Doc paths in the changed hunks are now host-qualified (`/mnt/taurus/data2/...final8.json`), addressing the prior AGENTS.md complaint. Note the verification log commands still use bare `/mnt/data2/...` — harmless (log, not doc), but the cited doc path and the command that produced it differ by the `taurus/` prefix, so reproducibility depends on a symlink.

# Possible false positives (do not re-raise)
- The renormalized-confidence-clears-`min_confidence` concern from the prior pass is genuinely constrained for the audio-only *probe* path now: the guard requires raw `top_score ≥ 0.50`, raw margin `≥ 0.08`, ≥2 positive domains, and top-raw-domain == target, evaluated before the confidence check. `test_audio_only_contested_probe_does_not_false_switch_on_small_raw_margin` exercises the margin rejection.
- The `return_query_window_embeddings` gating is safe: the only consumer (`omni._process_batch` → `query_window_embeddings[idx]`) is itself gated on `auto_glossary_enabled`, which is what sets the flag; no other reader of `RetrievalResult.query_window_embeddings` exists in the packet, so non-auto sessions losing the field is not a regression.
- Guard fields default correctly in `RouterConfig`, so routers built in tests without passing them (e.g. `test_cached_probe_scores_can_confirm_audio_only_switch`) still enforce 0.50/0.08/2.
- `_audio_probe_guard` is computed before the if/elif chain but consumed only in the audio-only elif; the `unsupported_current` target reassignment does not corrupt it.

# Final recommendation
Mergeable with low risk as a scoped guard. Before merge, prefer to (1) close the centroid-only audio-only bypass (Should-fix #1) so no lone renormalized audio signal — probe *or* centroid — can clear `min_confidence` unguarded, and (2) add or explicitly defer an agent-level test that drives the `return_query_window_embeddings` + probe path through the real `MaxSimRetrievalPlugin`. The `min_raw_margin=0.08` vs measured ~0.01 deltas means the audio-only feature ships effectively inert; that is acceptable only because the docs frame it as a fallback and no eval claims otherwise — do not later cite the synthetic-probe fixture runs as evidence that audio-only production switching works.

```

```text
# Verdict
NEEDS_FIX

The change under review is `368262d → a5ed4ff` ("Add E2E generated-target glossary routing"): it fills in the previously no-op `_after_translation_tick` to write generated target text into `router_text_window`/`router_text_source`, drops the `common_terms` base slice (`base_slice: none`, `type: diagnostic`), simplifies `_autoterm_base_preset`, and adds Chinese topic keywords for nlp/medicine only. The base-slice removal and the external-source guard are correct and tested. But the generated-target routing path has a real functional gap for two of the four advertised domains, a precision/self-reinforcement risk that is untested, and its central correctness claim ("one routing tick behind") cannot be confirmed from the packet.

# Must fix before merge

### 1. Generated-target routing cannot switch to finance/legal for a Chinese target (silent dead path)
- **Severity:** High (spec mismatch / hidden functional gap)
- **Where:** `framework/agents/term_memory/domain_taxonomy.py` `DOMAIN_TOPIC_KEYWORDS`; consumed by `topic_keyword_scores` → `HybridWindowTopicRouter._score_hybrid`.
- **Why real:** The default `auto_glossary_presets` is `nlp_core_10k,medicine_core_10k,finance_core_10k,legal_core_10k`, and the new production signal is the *generated target* window, which for the default `English -> Chinese` pair is Chinese. This commit adds Chinese keywords to the `nlp` and `medicine` blocks only. The `finance` and `legal` blocks remain English-only (`\bmarket(s)?\b`, `\bcourt(s)?\b`, …). Python `\b`-anchored English regex never matches Chinese text, so `text_topic_score` for finance/legal is identically 0 on any Chinese generated target. The router therefore can never route *to* finance or legal via the generated-target path — the exact "deployable E2E route" this change is built to provide. The docs and paper wording claim the router "switches the active domain slice" among the domain inventory without stating that two of the four domains are unreachable through the shipping signal.
- **How to verify:** Feed a Chinese finance/legal generated-target window (e.g. 市场/股票/利率 or 法院/合同/管辖权) through `HybridWindowTopicRouter.observe(..., router_text_source="generated_target")` from a `finance`/`legal` starting state; confirm `text_topic_score` and any switch. There is no such test in `test_hybrid_window_topic_router.py` (only the nlp→medicine Chinese case).
- **Minimal fix direction:** Add Chinese finance/legal topic keywords symmetric with nlp/medicine, or explicitly scope the E2E generated-target claim/docs to the domains that actually have target-language coverage.

### 2. "One routing tick behind" guarantee is unverifiable and is the correctness hinge of the feature
- **Severity:** High if the call ordering is wrong (self-reinforcement becomes immediate)
- **Where:** `framework/agents/omni.py` `_after_translation_tick` (writes `router_text_window`) vs `_observe_active_glossary` (reads it and drives the router). The call site of `_after_translation_tick` within the streaming loop is **not in the packet** (`omni.py` truncated).
- **Why real:** The docs assert "The generated target window is one routing tick behind the current chunk, so a chunk's own translation cannot influence its own glossary retrieval." That property holds only if `_after_translation_tick` runs *after* `_observe_active_glossary` for the same chunk. If it runs before (or in the same pass that then re-routes), the current chunk's own translation — produced under the currently active glossary — feeds the domain decision for that chunk, closing a self-reinforcing loop with no guardrail. The method was previously a `return None` stub already invoked somewhere, so the call exists; the ordering does not.
- **How to verify:** `grep -n "_after_translation_tick" framework/agents/omni.py` and confirm it is invoked strictly after the per-chunk `_observe_active_glossary`, and that `session.history` at that point holds emitted *target translations* (not source/messages). Neither is confirmable from the packet.
- **Minimal fix direction:** None if ordering is already correct; if not, move the write after routing. Either way, add a test that asserts the current chunk's translation only affects the *next* chunk's `router_text_window`.

# Should fix

### 3. Generated target gets the lenient 2-window "with_text" threshold despite being a self-biased signal
- **Where:** `HybridWindowTopicRouter.observe` — `has_text = router_text and text_source != "none"`; generated_target ⇒ `has_text=True` ⇒ `min_consistent_windows_with_text` (2), and it bypasses the `_audio_probe_guard` (which only fires on `not has_text and has_probe`).
- **Why real:** Source transcript text is domain ground truth; generated target text is produced under the currently active (possibly wrong) glossary and can echo its domain vocabulary. Treating it with the same 2-window, no-raw-evidence-floor path as trusted source text is the weakest point for self-reinforcement the task explicitly flagged. With the renormalization introduced earlier on this branch, a single active text signal renormalizes `conf` toward its top-normalized value, so two windows of generic keyword hits can clear `min_confidence=0.60`.
- **Minimal fix direction:** Give `generated_target` its own (stricter) consistency/confidence treatment distinct from `manifest_source`, or require a raw-evidence floor before a generated-target-only signal can switch.

### 4. Several new Chinese keywords are high-frequency generic words → precision loss, biased toward the default NLP slice
- **Where:** `domain_taxonomy.py` new entries: nlp `注意力|嵌入|预训练|微调|提示` (0.9), `标注|解析|...` (1.0); medicine `试验|...` (1.0).
- **Why real:** `提示` (prompt/hint) and `解析`/`微调` are common in general and medical Chinese ("结果提示…"), and `试验` is generic. Because the default active slice is `nlp_core_10k`, spurious NLP keyword hits combine with the `min_current_margin` guard (which favors staying) to make it harder to *leave* NLP and easier to falsely score NLP on non-NLP audio. No test exercises noisy/realistic Chinese generated text — only one hand-built clean medicine sentence.

# Missing tests / benchmarks
- No agent-level test that a written `router_text_window`/`generated_target` actually flows through `_observe_active_glossary` into a router switch on the *following* chunk (the one-tick-behind contract, item 2).
- No finance/legal generated-target routing test (item 1) — the missing coverage hides that the path is dead there.
- No false-switch/self-reinforcement regression on realistic noisy Chinese generated text (item 3/4); `test_generated_target_chinese_topic_switches_after_two_windows` uses a keyword-dense clean sentence and cannot surface precision loss.
- No test that `session.history` semantics (target vs source) match what `_after_translation_tick` assumes.

# Performance risks
- None material. `_after_translation_tick` is a bounded string join over ≤`window` history items on the CPU path; not a retriever/GPU hot path.

# Spec mismatch / surprise changes
- Docs/README/paper wording present generated-target E2E routing as switching among the domain inventory, but the shipping Chinese-target signal only functions for nlp/medicine (item 1).
- `base_slice: none` + `common_terms type: diagnostic` correctly removes the common base from the active inventory (matches acceptance criteria), and `_active_retrieval_slices` returning only the domain slice is tested. Note `slice_role_for_preset("common_10k")` still returns `"base"` in the registry (`test_common_preset_maps_to_common_terms_slice`) — harmless only because `common_10k` is no longer in the active inventory; it is an internal inconsistency, not a bug in this path.
- Cited eval artifacts (`..._final8.json`) are now host-qualified per AGENTS.md, but are run results not present in the packet and remain unverifiable (pre-existing).

# Possible false positives
- The external-source guard (`current_source not in {"none","generated_target"}`) correctly preserves `manifest_source`/`streaming_asr` and is directly tested (`test_generated_target_translation_does_not_override_external_router_text`); the acceptance criterion "generated target must not override explicit external router_text" is met.
- The current-text dedup (`texts[-1] != current_text`) correctly avoids double-appending when `history` already contains the just-emitted translation; not a bug.
- Dropping the `type=="base"` scan in `_autoterm_base_preset` does not resurrect surprising legacy behavior: with `base_slice` present-and-empty or absent it returns the `"none"` default; `common_terms` is `diagnostic`, so it is never auto-selected as a base.
- `_meta_bool(enable_generated_target_text, True)` defaulting True is intentional and matches the yaml.

# Final recommendation
Do not merge as-is. Before merge: (1) add Chinese finance/legal topic keywords or scope the E2E claim to the covered domains; (2) confirm — with a test — that `_after_translation_tick` runs after per-chunk routing and that `session.history` holds target translations, so the one-tick-behind/no-self-influence property actually holds; (3) treat `generated_target` more conservatively than trusted source text (stricter consistency or a raw-evidence floor) and add a noisy-Chinese false-switch regression. Items 1 (partially), 2, and the `session.history` semantics cannot be fully confirmed from the packet because the `omni.py` call site is truncated.

```
## .codex/reviews/claude-review-20260706-233656.md

Current file excerpt/full content, possibly truncated:
```text
# Verdict
NEEDS_FIX

The change under review is `368472d → 7449b53` (`Add E2E generated-target glossary routing` + `Harden generated-target glossary routing`). It fills in the previously no-op `_after_translation_tick` to write generated target text into `router_text_window`/`router_text_source`, drops `common_terms` from the default active inventory (`base_slice: none`, `type: diagnostic`), simplifies `_autoterm_base_preset`, adds a stricter `min_consistent_windows_generated_target=3` path, and adds Chinese topic keywords for **all four** domains. The prior review's two hardest items (finance/legal Chinese keywords, and lenient 2-window threshold for generated target) are genuinely closed here. What remains are two unverifiable correctness hinges and precision/benchmark gaps.

# Must fix before merge

### 1. The "one routing tick behind" / no-self-influence property is unverifiable from the packet and is the correctness hinge
- **Severity:** High if the call ordering is wrong.
- **Where:** `framework/agents/omni.py` `_after_translation_tick` (writes `router_text_window`) vs `_observe_active_glossary` (reads it). The call site of `_after_translation_tick` inside the streaming/batch loop is **not in the packet** (`omni.py` truncated).
- **Why real:** `docs/adaptive_working_glossary.md` asserts "The generated target window is one routing tick behind the current chunk, so a chunk's own translation cannot influence its own glossary retrieval." That holds only if `_after_translation_tick` runs strictly *after* the per-chunk `_observe_active_glossary`. If it runs before (or in the same routing pass), the current chunk's own translation — produced under the possibly-wrong active glossary — feeds that chunk's domain decision, closing a self-reinforcing loop with no guardrail. The added test `test_generated_target_text_is_used_by_next_router_tick_only` hand-sequences `observe → after_tick → observe`; it proves the flow-through in mock but does **not** prove the production loop orders the two calls that way.
- **How to verify:** `grep -n "_after_translation_tick" framework/agents/omni.py`; confirm it is invoked strictly after the per-chunk `_observe_active_glossary`. Add a test that drives the real per-chunk path and asserts a chunk's translation only affects the *next* chunk's `router_text_window`.
- **Minimal fix direction:** None if ordering is already correct; otherwise move the write after routing.

### 2. `_after_translation_tick` assumes `session.history` holds target translations; this is unconfirmed
- **Severity:** High if `history` holds source/messages.
- **Where:** `_after_translation_tick` — `texts = [... for item in session.history[-window:] ...]`.
- **Why real:** The whole feature depends on `session.history` containing *emitted target translations* (Chinese). If it holds source-side text, message dicts, or interleaved source+target, `text_topic_score` is computed over the wrong content and the generated-target route is silently miscalibrated. `OmniSession.history: List[str]` is declared but what is appended to it is not in the packet.
- **How to verify:** Inspect every `session.history.append(...)` in `omni.py`; confirm it appends the target translation string at the point `_after_translation_tick` reads it, and that the caller's append vs the internal dedup (`texts[-1] != current_text`) don't double-count.

# Should fix

### 3. Several new Chinese keywords are high-frequency/dual-use → precision loss biased toward the default NLP slice
- **Where:** `domain_taxonomy.py` new entries, e.g. nlp `提示|微调|解析` (`提示`="hint/indicate" is common in general and clinical Chinese: "结果提示…"; `解析` is generic), medicine `试验` (generic "trial/experiment"), medicine `核磁|磁共振|CT` marked `case_sensitive=True` (irrelevant for CJK, harmless but sloppy).
- **Why real:** Because the default active slice is `nlp_core_10k`, spurious NLP keyword hits combine with `min_current_margin` (which favors staying) to make it both easier to falsely retain NLP on non-NLP audio and harder to leave. No test exercises noisy/realistic Chinese generated text — only hand-built keyword-dense clean sentences — so precision loss cannot surface.
- **Minimal fix direction:** Drop the most generic tokens or lower their weights; add a noisy-Chinese ACL-only regression asserting `switch_count == 0`.

### 4. Renormalized single-signal confidence still saturates `min_confidence` on the generated-target-only path
- **Where:** `topic_router.py` `_score_hybrid` renormalization (introduced earlier on this branch) + `observe`: `generated_target ⇒ has_text=True`, bypassing `_audio_probe_guard`.
- **Why real:** In the shipping config the generated-target text is often the only active text signal; renormalization drives `conf` toward its top-normalized value, so ~3 windows of generic keyword hits can clear `min_confidence=0.60`. The 3-window consistency guard is the *only* added protection for a signal the task explicitly flags as self-biased; there is no raw-evidence floor as there is for the probe path. Given items 3 and the default NLP bias, this is where a false switch would appear.

# Missing tests / benchmarks
- No test drives the real per-chunk streaming loop to confirm the one-tick-behind contract (item 1) or `session.history` target semantics (item 2).
- No noisy/realistic Chinese generated-target false-switch regression (items 3/4). The four `test_generated_target_chinese_*` tests all use clean keyword-dense single sentences and cannot fail on precision.
- No end-to-end run of the generated-target route exists. All cited artifacts (`..._final8.json`) are router-unit **source-text** diagnostics; the docs themselves say generated-target E2E eval is still future work. Yet the paper wording presents generated-target windows as "the deployable E2E path." The deployable claim is wired but unbenchmarked.

# Performance risks
- None material in this diff. `_after_translation_tick` is a bounded CPU string join over ≤`window` history items, off the retriever/GPU hot path. (The probe re-encode/lock concerns from prior passes live below the review base `368472d` and are out of scope here.)

# Spec mismatch / surprise changes
- `base_slice: none` + `common_terms type: diagnostic` correctly removes the common base from the active inventory and `_active_retrieval_slices` returns only the domain slice (`test_auto_active_retrieval_uses_domain_specific_slice_only`) — matches acceptance criteria. Note the residual inconsistency: `slice_role_for_preset("common_10k")` still returns `"base"` in `slice_registry` (`test_common_preset_maps_to_common_terms_slice`). Harmless only because `common_10k` is no longer in the active inventory; it is an internal inconsistency, not a bug in this path.
- Paper/README wording claims generated-target E2E routing as the shipping route while no E2E evidence exists (see Missing benchmarks).
- `_autoterm_base_preset` no longer scans for `type=="base"`; with `base_slice` present-and-`none` it returns `"none"`, and `common_terms` (now `diagnostic`) is never auto-selected — no resurrected legacy behavior.

# Possible false positives (do not re-raise)
- **The prior Must-fix "finance/legal unreachable for Chinese target" is fixed:** finance/legal Chinese keywords are added, and `_router_all_domains` in `test_hybrid_window_topic_router.py` exercises finance→ and legal→ switches. Do not re-raise as a dead path.
- **The prior Should-fix "generated_target gets lenient 2-window threshold" is fixed:** `min_consistent_windows_generated_target=3` and the `is_generated_target` branch in `observe` apply the stricter path; unit-tested (`..._switches_after_three_windows`).
- The external-source guard (`current_source not in {"none","generated_target"}`) correctly preserves `manifest_source`/`streaming_asr` and is directly tested; the "must not override external router_text" criterion is met.
- The current-text dedup (`texts[-1] != current_text`) correctly avoids double-appending when `history` already holds the just-emitted translation.
- `enable_generated_target_text`/`generated_target_window_chunks`/`generated_target_min_chars` are typed yaml/config fields (not env-var controls), consistent with the workstation constraint.

# Final recommendation
Do not merge as-is. Before merge: (1) confirm — with a test on the real streaming loop, not hand-sequenced method calls — that `_after_translation_tick` runs after per-chunk routing and reads target translations from `session.history`, so the one-tick-behind/no-self-influence property actually holds; (2) add a noisy realistic Chinese generated-target regression asserting zero false switches, and trim the most generic new keywords or give the generated-target-only path a raw-evidence floor rather than relying solely on the 3-window guard; (3) stop presenting generated-target routing as the validated deployable E2E path until an end-to-end run exists, or explicitly scope the claim to "wired, not yet E2E-benchmarked." Items 1 and 2 cannot be fully confirmed from the packet because the `omni.py` call site and `history` append points are truncated.
```

```text
# Verdict
NEEDS_FIX

The change under review is `368472d → 22fd011` (`Add E2E generated-target glossary routing`, `Harden generated-target glossary routing`, `Document and test generated-target routing guards`). It fills in the previously no-op `_after_translation_tick`, drops `common_terms` from the default active inventory, adds Chinese topic keywords for all four domains, adds a stricter `min_consistent_windows_generated_target=3` path, and adds docs + tests. Several prior-review items are genuinely closed here (finance/legal Chinese keywords now present and tested; stricter generated-target consistency; honest "E2E benchmark pending" caveats). What remains is a real guardrail gap that is the explicit subject of the task, plus test/verification weaknesses on the correctness-critical properties.

# Must fix before merge

### 1. Generated-target routing has no raw-evidence floor; the self-reinforcement guard the task asked for is not actually implemented
- **Severity:** Medium–High (robustness / spec of the feature's whole novelty)
- **Where:** `framework/agents/term_memory/topic_router.py` `HybridWindowTopicRouter.observe` — `is_generated_target` only selects `min_consistent_windows_generated_target` (3); the `_audio_probe_guard` (`not has_text and has_probe`) is bypassed for generated target because `has_text=True`.
- **Why real:** The task explicitly asks "whether using generated target text can self-reinforce wrong glossary choices without enough guardrails." The only added protection over trusted source text is one extra consistency window (3 vs 2). Generated target text is produced under the currently-active (possibly wrong) glossary, so its keyword content is biased toward the current domain. Unlike the audio-only probe path — which requires a raw top-score ≥ 0.50, raw margin ≥ 0.08, and ≥2 positive domains before a renormalized score may switch — the generated-target path has no analogous absolute-evidence floor. Because the branch upstream renormalizes over present signals (documented in `docs/adaptive_working_glossary.md`), a single active text signal can drive `conf` toward its top-normalized value and clear `min_confidence=0.60`, so ~3 windows of biased keyword hits can switch, and `min_current_margin` simultaneously makes it *harder to leave* a wrong initial slice. The dominant realistic failure is sticky retention of the wrong (default `nlp`) slice, which no guard or test addresses.
- **How to verify:** Drive `observe(..., router_text_source="generated_target")` from an `nlp` start with target text that echoes NLP terms while the underlying content is medicine; confirm whether the router can (a) falsely retain nlp or (b) switch on generic biased hits. No such regression exists.
- **Minimal fix direction:** Give `generated_target` an explicit raw-evidence/margin floor before it can reach switch confidence (parallel to `_audio_probe_guard`), and/or add a realistic noisy regression asserting the intended behavior; do not rely solely on the 3-window count.

### 2. The one-tick-behind / no-self-influence property is guaranteed only by a brittle source-substring test
- **Severity:** Medium (correctness hinge, weakly protected)
- **Where:** `test_auto_working_fixed_top10.py::test_streaming_loop_orders_routing_before_generated_target_write`; the actual streaming-loop call sites in `framework/agents/omni.py` are truncated in the packet.
- **Why real:** The docs assert "a chunk's own translation cannot influence its own glossary retrieval," which holds only if `_observe_active_glossary` (inside `_retrieve_batch`) runs before `_after_translation_tick` (inside `_generate_one`/`_generate_batch`) for the same chunk. The added test enforces this via `source.index(...)` string-position comparisons — a structural heuristic that breaks silently on any refactor that reorders code textually without changing runtime order, and cannot observe the actual control flow. It also does not prove `_after_translation_tick` is invoked *only* in the generate path, nor that `session.history` contains only emitted target translations (it is only inferred from `append(text)` preceding `after_translation_tick(text=text)`).
- **How to verify:** Confirm from the untruncated loop that observe precedes after-tick per chunk, and add a runtime test (mock loop) asserting chunk N's translation only affects chunk N+1's `router_text_window` — the hand-sequenced `test_generated_target_text_is_used_by_next_router_tick_only` calls the methods manually and does not exercise the loop.
- **Minimal fix direction:** Add a mock end-to-end streaming assertion; keep the string test only as a supplement.

# Should fix

- **`session.history` content semantics unconfirmed.** `_after_translation_tick` reads `session.history[-window:]` as generated target text. If history is appended anywhere outside the generate path with source/message content, `text_topic_score` is computed over the wrong content. Only inferred from the two generate-path appends; verify no other `session.history.append` interleaves non-translation strings.
- **`slice_role_for_preset("common_10k")` still returns `"base"`** (`test_common_preset_maps_to_common_terms_slice`) while the config marks `common_terms` `type: diagnostic` and drops it from the active inventory. Harmless in the active path but an internal inconsistency now that `base_slice: none`.
- **`核磁|磁共振|CT` medicine keyword:** `CT` in a CJK regex has no word boundary and matches any substring; on mixed-language target text it can match inside unrelated tokens. Low impact (target is Chinese) but sloppy for a case-insensitive bare `CT`.

# Missing tests / benchmarks
- No realistic noisy/self-reinforcement regression for generated target (item 1). The four `test_generated_target_chinese_*` tests all use clean keyword-dense single sentences; the sole noise test (`..._noisy_generic_chinese_does_not_switch_to_nlp`) is one generic sentence checking non-switch, not a wrong-glossary bias case.
- No runtime streaming-loop test of the one-tick-behind contract (item 2).
- No end-to-end generated-target switch-quality run exists; the docs themselves now state this is pending. Cited `..._final8.json` artifacts are source-text router-unit diagnostics, correctly labeled as upper bounds.

# Performance risks
- None material in this diff. `_after_translation_tick` is a bounded CPU string join over ≤`window` history items, off the retriever/GPU path. No TP/PP, scheduling, or cache interaction. (Probe re-encode/lock concerns from earlier reviews live below base `368472d` and are out of scope.)

# Spec mismatch / surprise changes
- `base_slice: none` + `common_terms type: diagnostic` correctly removes the common base; `_active_retrieval_slices` returning only the domain slice is tested (`test_auto_active_retrieval_uses_domain_specific_slice_only`). `_autoterm_base_preset` no longer scans for `type=="base"`; with `base_slice` present-and-`none` it returns `"none"`, and `common_terms` (diagnostic) is never auto-selected — no resurrected legacy behavior. Matches acceptance criteria.
- README/paper wording presents the generated-target route as "the wired production path" but is now appropriately caveated ("End-to-end generated-target benchmarking is still pending"; "Full E2E generated-target switch quality remains a pending benchmark"). This is honest, but note the shipping primary signal is generated target (no ASR), and audio-only probe switching remains effectively inert on real audio given `audio_probe_min_raw_margin=0.08` vs the ~0.01 real deltas the repo's own probe doc reports — so the initial slice dominates until translations accumulate.

# Possible false positives (do not re-raise)
- The prior "finance/legal unreachable for Chinese target" is fixed: Chinese finance/legal keywords added and exercised by `_router_all_domains` finance/legal switch tests.
- The prior "generated_target gets lenient 2-window threshold" is fixed: `min_consistent_windows_generated_target=3` plumbed yaml → `OmniConfig` → `RouterConfig` and unit-tested.
- The external-source guard (`current_source not in {"none","generated_target"}`) correctly preserves `manifest_source`/`streaming_asr` and is directly tested — acceptance criterion "must not override external router_text" met.
- The current-text dedup (`texts[-1] != current_text`) correctly avoids double-appending when history already holds the just-emitted translation.
- `enable_generated_target_text`/`generated_target_window_chunks`/`generated_target_min_chars` are typed yaml/config fields (not env-var controls), consistent with the workstation constraint.
- The generic Chinese tokens flagged in an earlier packet (`提示`/`解析`) are **not** present in this HEAD's `domain_taxonomy.py` diff; do not re-raise them.

# Final recommendation
Do not merge as-is. Before merge: (1) add a real guardrail for the generated-target-only path — an absolute raw-evidence/margin floor analogous to `_audio_probe_guard`, not just the 3-window count — since a stricter consistency count alone does not answer the task's explicit self-reinforcement question; (2) add a mock streaming-loop test that proves the one-tick-behind property at runtime and confirm `session.history` holds only target translations, rather than relying on the brittle source-substring ordering test; (3) add a realistic noisy/wrong-glossary Chinese generated-target regression. Items depending on the truncated `omni.py` streaming loop (exact observe/after-tick ordering and `history` append sites) cannot be fully confirmed from the packet.
```
